I just signed up for a storage unit at the end of last week. I compared this place to 3 other storage facilities in the area and decided on this one. For 3 reasons...

1. I like that it's clean and spacious. Not just when you come in to park, the lobby and the driveway to the storage area. In comparison to the other places I looked at, this one looked the best.
2. There is a huge lobby area with everything you can possibly need from tape, boxes, mattress/couch covers, bubble wrap, etc.
3. Kristyn helped me find the storage unit for me and was super helpful. She never pressured me to take the unit right away and even allowed me to compare other facilities to show that her facility did indeed have the best rates in the area.

We haven't put things in storage yet as I got really busy, but will do so soon.

So far a good facility to rent storage at!<//Review>

<Rate>5<//Rate>< review>
Great food rivaling some of the more expensive Indian restaurants in the area.
Great service, great people who aim to make sure you receive a great meal at a great price.
A treasure located in a very non-descript and modest strip mall.
I do not believe you will be disappointed but be careful with some of the dishes as they are made fresh and may be a little spicy at times.
They have sweet lassie which is made fresh but you have to order it while the mango and rose lassi are also made fresh but are in the cooler.  I discovered them when my son told us about them, they have become a couple of times a week habit.</review>

< Review>
Good organic coffee, fair trade. Not as affordable as your "gourmet" grocery store coffee (Starbucks, Peets, etc) but I'm willing to pay a premium to know that the farmers aren't getting stiffed. Most of their beans run from $14 to $18 a pound, light to dark roast, and they have a few decaf options.

Not a coffee shop - they only sell beans and coffee accessories (grinders,  french presses, etc). Warehouse setting, it looks like they do all their roasting and packaging on premises, but I haven't clarified. They do have pre-packaged beans available, but it's a better deal to fill a bag yourself - I think the pre-packaged beans are only 10 oz but cost as much as a pound of the bulk coffee. They also have half pound bags which is nice if you don't want to commit to a whole pound of something you've never tired before.<//Review>

We have been dine in only customers for years. Due to the new safer at home restrictions, we have been cooking at home. Tonight, we needed a break. We ordered through their website, and our food was ready in 25 minutes. It was even better than the last time we dined in. My chicken wrap was moist, and the salad was super fresh. The gyro wrap was full of tender lamb and the mixed kebabs were perfectly cooked. The fries and rice were perfect too. Everything was packaged nicely and as always the service was friendly. I highly recommend this local spot.</review>

<Rate>5< /Rate><gmap_id>0x80c2bb777755eec5:0x339bb862084b8a9f<//gmap_id><resp>None< /resp>< review>
I  love this place without a doubt. Clean dining area and spacious. I always go here for dinner when I stay at work late. I always order the same plate which is number 28 on their menu a mix of three different meats (chicken, beef, and lamb), jasmine rice, salad, hummus, and pita bread. The combo and it always satisfies me every time I order it; its a big plate for big eaters such as myself. The have vegan options too for vegan eaters or health conscious folks. They are fast too so do not worry waiting too long. Great customer service, they bring the food to you. Bathroom is not the best but I mainly go for the food which they have not disappoint. Recommend colleagues to check this place out.< /review>

We stumbled onto this gem via google maps after our visit to whole foods (we're visitors from Singapore) and we loved it! Tacos are $1.25 each, and there was a short but fast moving queue when they opened for business at 5pm. The intestines and stomachs tacos were my favourite if you're into them.
